viewBox="0 0 16 16"><path fill="currentColor" d="M2.473 10.86a.7.7 0 0 0-.22-.14.67.67 0 0 0-.507 0 .7.7 0 0 0-.22.14.7.7 0 0 0-.14.22.67.67 0 0 0 .14.727q.099.089.22.14a.63.63 0 0 0 .507 0 .8.8 0 0 0 .506q.05.123.14.22.097.09.22.14a.63.63 0 0 0 .506 0 .8.8 0 0 0 .22-.14.8.8 0 0 0 .14-.22.63.63 0 0 0 0-.506.7.7 0 0 0-.14-.22M14 7.333H4.667a.667.667 0 0 0 0 1.334H14a.667.667 0 1 0 0-1.334M2.473 building</div></div></a><a class="text-button text-center py-1" href="https://ui.tinybird.co/login">Sign In</a></div></div></div></nav></aside><main class="w-full grow pt-6 pb-6 md:pt-8 sm:pb-8 md:max-w-[calc(100%_-var(--sidebar-width))]" data-pagefind-body=""><div class="hidden sm:block relative max-w-7xl mx-auto px-5 md:px-6 "><nav aria-label="Breadcrumb" class="py-4 max-w-4xl md:px-4 mb-2"><ol class="flex items-center text-sm"><li><a class="hover:font-semibold hover:underline hover:text-black" href="/docs/forward/get-started/quickstarts">Home</a></li></ol></nav></div><div class="relative max-w-7xl mx-auto px-5 md:px-6 xl:grid xl:grid-cols-[1fr_280px]"><div class="max-w-4xl text-body md:px-4 md:pb-20 relative" role="main"><article><div class="flex flex-col sm:flex-row sm:items-center justify-between gap-4 mb-6"><h1 id="how-to-debug-queries-using-system-query-log" class="t-h3" data-pagefind-weight="20.0">How to debug queries using system.query_log<a class="headerlink" href="#how-to-debug-queries-using-system-query-log" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h1><div class="flex-shrink-0 w-auto"><div class="relative inline-block w-auto" data-pagefind-ignore="true"><div class="flex rounded-md overflow-hidden border border-v-border-02 hover:border-v-border-03 transition-colors"><button class="flex items-center gap-1.5 px-3 py-1.5 text-sm transition-colors min-w-[106px] text-v-text-01"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="24" height="24" fill="none" stroke="currentColor" stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" stroke-width="2" viewBox="0 0 24 24" class="w-4 h-4 dark:invert-[0.85] dark:brightness-[0.9]"><path d="M14 2H6a2 2 0 0 0-2 2v16a2 2 0 0 0 2 2h12a2 2 0 0 0 2-2V8z"></path><path d="M14 2v6h6M16 13H8M16 17H8M10 9H8"></path></svg><span>Copy as MD</span></button><button class="flex items-center justify-center px-2 py-1.5 text-sm text-v-text-01 border-l border-v-border-02 min-w-[32px]" aria-haspopup="true" aria-expanded="false"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" fill="none" class="w-3 h-3 dark:invert-[0.85] dark:brightness-[0.9]" style="margin-top:-4px;margin-left:-4px"><path fill="currentColor" d="M8.1 11.41 4 6.995 4.745 6 8.1 9.795 11.454 6l.746.994z"></path></svg></button></div></div></div></div><p>When troubleshooting performance issues or investigating query failures, you often need execution details beyond what standard monitoring provides.  The <code>system.query_log</code> table is a native ClickHouse system table that records query execution at the database engine level beneath Tinybird.<!-- --> <!-- -->It stores detailed information for every query executed in your Workspace, including execution time, memory usage, error codes, and failure reasons. For a complete description of available columns and data types, see the ClickHouse documentation on the <a href="https://clickhouse.com/docs/operations/system-tables/query_log" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer" class="inline-flex items-center"><code>system.query_log</code></a> table.</p><div class="my-4 flex items-start gap-2 py-3 px-4 rounded border border-v-border bg-v-callout-info text-code"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 16 16" class="inline shrink-0 mt-px h-5"><path fill="currentColor" d="M7.86 9.742a1 1 0 0 0-.08.1.5.5 0 0 0-.06.12.4.4 0 0 0-.04.12 1 1 0 0 0 0 .134.56.56 0 0 0 .053.253.6.6 0 0 0 .36.36.63.63 0 0 0 .507 0 .6.6 0 0 0 .36-.36.7.7 0 0 0 .04-.253.667.667 0 0 0-1.14-.474m.473-8.86a6.667 6.667 0 1 0 0 13.334 6.667 6.667 0 0 0 0-13.334m0 12a5.333 5.333 0 1 1 0-10.666 5.333 5.333 0 0 1 0 10.666m0-8.666a2 2 0 0 0-1.733 1 .667.667 0 1 0 1.153.666.667.667 0 0 1 1.052-.138.667.667 0 0 1-.472 1.138.667.667 0 0 0-.666.667v.667a.667.667 0 0 0 1.333 0v-.12a2 2 0 0 0-.667-3.88"></path></svg><div class="text-v-text"><p><strong>When should I use system.query_log?</strong></p><p>Use <code>system.query_log</code> when you need to:</p><ul><li>Debug queries that are slower than expected</li><li>Investigate why specific queries are failing</li><li>Analyze memory consumption patterns</li><li>Track which Endpoints consume the most resources</li><li>Correlate query execution with Endpoint performance metrics</li></ul><p>For routine monitoring of Endpoint performance, use <a href="./analyze-endpoints-performance"><code>tinybird.pipe_stats_rt</code></a> instead.</p></div></div><p>Read on to learn how to safely query <code>system.query_log</code> and use it to solve real-world debugging challenges.</p><h2 id="before-you-start" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">Before you start<a class="headerlink" href="#before-you-start" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><p>The <code>system.query_log</code> table is a ClickHouse system table that contains extensive historical data. Before querying it, understand:</p><ul><li>How to <a href="./analyze-endpoints-performance">analyze Endpoint performance</a> using <code>tinybird.pipe_stats_rt</code></li><li>Basic SQL query patterns in Tinybird</li></ul><div class="my-4 flex items-start gap-2 py-3 px-4 rounded border border-v-border bg-v-callout-warning text-error"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 24 24" class="inline shrink-0 mt-px h-5"><path fill="currentColor" fill-rule="evenodd" d="M12 1.25C6.063 1.25 1.25 6.063 1.25 12S6.063 22.75 12 22.75 22.75 17.937 22.75 12 17.937 1.25 12 1.25M2.75 12A9.25 9.25 0 0 1 12 2.75c2.284 0 4.376.828 5.99 2.2l-.02.02-13 13-.02.02A9.2 9.2 0 0 1 2.75 12m3.26 7.05A9.25 9.25 0 0 0 19.05 6.01l-.019.02-13 13z" clip-rule="evenodd"></path></svg><div class="text-v-text"><p>The <code>system.query_log</code> table contains all historical query data. <strong>Always filter by <code>event_time</code></strong> to avoid slow queries or timeouts. Queries without time filters can take hundreds of seconds or timeout completely. <strong>Never run</strong> <code>SELECT * FROM system.query_log</code> without filtering by time.</p></div></div><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-header"><div class="snippet-headerInfo overflow"><h5 class="snippet-title as-font--caption-bold as-cap overflow mr-4" title="Safe query pattern with 1-hour lookback">Safe query pattern with 1-hour lookback</h5></div></div><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT *
FROM system.query_log
WHERE event_time &gt;= now() - INTERVAL 1 HOUR
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>Start with a 1-hour window (typically 1-2 seconds to execute) and expand the time range only if needed.</p><h2 id="understand-query-lifecycle" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">Understand query lifecycle<a class="headerlink" href="#understand-query-lifecycle" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><p>Every query in Tinybird generates two entries in <code>system.query_log</code>:</p><ol><li><strong>QueryStart</strong> - Logged when query execution begins</li><li><strong>QueryFinish</strong> - Logged when the query completes successfully</li></ol><p>If a query fails, you&#x27;ll see a different type instead of <code>QueryFinish</code>:</p><ul><li><strong>ExceptionBeforeStart</strong> - Query failed before execution started (usually syntax errors)</li><li><strong>ExceptionWhileProcessing</strong> - Query failed during execution (timeouts, memory exceeded, runtime errors)</li></ul><p>Here&#x27;s how the query lifecycle flows:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">┌─────────────────┐
│  Query Begins   │
└────────┬────────┘
         │
         ▼
    QueryStart ──────────────────┐
         │                       │
         │                       │
         ▼                       ▼
┌─────────────────┐     ┌──────────────────────┐
│ Query Executes  │     │  Syntax/Init Error   │
└────────┬────────┘     └──────────┬───────────┘
         │                         │
         │                         ▼
         │              ExceptionBeforeStart
         │
    ┌────┴────┐
    │         │
    ▼         ▼
 Success   Runtime Error
    │         │
    ▼         ▼
QueryFinish   ExceptionWhileProcessing
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>This two-entry pattern helps you distinguish between queries that are still running and those that have finished or failed.</p><h2 id="common-debugging-scenarios" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">Common debugging scenarios<a class="headerlink" href="#common-debugging-scenarios" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><h3 id="find-slow-queries" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Find slow queries<a class="headerlink" href="#find-slow-queries" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>Identify queries taking longer than expected:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-header"><div class="snippet-headerInfo overflow"><h5 class="snippet-title as-font--caption-bold as-cap overflow mr-4" title="Queries taking more than 5 seconds">Queries taking more than 5 seconds</h5></div></div><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT
    event_time,
    query_id,
    JSONExtractString(log_comment, &#x27;pipe&#x27;) as pipe_name,
    query_duration_ms / 1000.0 as duration_seconds,
    formatReadableSize(memory_usage) as peak_memory,
    substring(query, 1, 100) as query_preview
FROM system.query_log
WHERE event_time &gt;= now() - INTERVAL 1 HOUR
    AND type = &#x27;QueryFinish&#x27;
    AND query_duration_ms &gt; 5000
ORDER BY query_duration_ms DESC
LIMIT 20
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>This helps you identify performance bottlenecks in your Endpoints or scheduled operations.</p><h3 id="investigate-query-failures" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Investigate query failures<a class="headerlink" href="#investigate-query-failures" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>Track which queries are failing and why:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-header"><div class="snippet-headerInfo overflow"><h5 class="snippet-title as-font--caption-bold as-cap overflow mr-4" title="Failed queries in the last hour">Failed queries in the last hour</h5></div></div><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT
    event_time,
    query_id,
    type,
    JSONExtractString(log_comment, &#x27;pipe&#x27;) as pipe_name,
    exception
FROM system.query_log
WHERE event_time &gt;= now() - INTERVAL 1 HOUR
    AND type IN (&#x27;ExceptionBeforeStart&#x27;, &#x27;ExceptionWhileProcessing&#x27;)
ORDER BY event_time DESC
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>The <code>exception</code> column contains the error message, helping you quickly identify syntax errors, timeouts, or resource limits.</p><h3 id="analyze-memory-consumption" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Analyze memory consumption<a class="headerlink" href="#analyze-memory-consumption" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>Find queries consuming the most memory:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-header"><div class="snippet-headerInfo overflow"><h5 class="snippet-title as-font--caption-bold as-cap overflow mr-4" title="Memory-intensive queries">Memory-intensive queries</h5></div></div><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT
    event_time,
    query_id,
    JSONExtractString(log_comment, &#x27;pipe&#x27;) as pipe_name,
    formatReadableSize(memory_usage) as peak_memory,
    query_duration_ms / 1000.0 as duration_seconds
FROM system.query_log
WHERE event_time &gt;= now() - INTERVAL 1 HOUR
    AND type = &#x27;QueryFinish&#x27;
ORDER BY memory_usage DESC
LIMIT 20
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>The <code>memory_usage</code> column shows peak memory in bytes. High memory usage may indicate opportunities for query optimization.</p><h3 id="track-query-failure-rates" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Track query failure rates<a class="headerlink" href="#track-query-failure-rates" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>Monitor how often queries are failing over time:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-header"><div class="snippet-headerInfo overflow"><h5 class="snippet-title as-font--caption-bold as-cap overflow mr-4" title="Query failures by hour">Query failures by hour</h5></div></div><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT
    toStartOfHour(event_time) as hour,
    type,
    count() as failure_count
FROM system.query_log
WHERE event_time &gt;= now() - INTERVAL 24 HOUR
    AND type IN (&#x27;ExceptionBeforeStart&#x27;, &#x27;ExceptionWhileProcessing&#x27;)
GROUP BY hour, type
ORDER BY hour DESC
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h2 id="connect-query-log-with-endpoint-stats" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">Connect query_log with Endpoint stats<a class="headerlink" href="#connect-query-log-with-endpoint-stats" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><p>The <code>query_id</code> in <code>system.query_log</code> matches the <code>request_id</code> from <code>tinybird.pipe_stats_rt</code>. This lets you combine high-level request metrics with detailed query execution data.</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-header"><div class="snippet-headerInfo overflow"><h5 class="snippet-title as-font--caption-bold as-cap overflow mr-4" title="Combine endpoint stats with query details">Combine endpoint stats with query details</h5></div></div><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT
    ps.pipe_name,
    ps.start_datetime,
    ps.duration as request_duration,
    formatReadableSize(ql.memory_usage) as query_memory,
    ql.type as execution_status
FROM tinybird.pipe_stats_rt ps
JOIN system.query_log ql ON ps.request_id = ql.query_id
WHERE ps.start_datetime &gt;= now() - INTERVAL 1 HOUR
    AND ql.type = &#x27;QueryFinish&#x27;
ORDER BY ps.start_datetime DESC
LIMIT 100
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><div class="my-4 flex items-start gap-2 py-3 px-4 rounded border border-v-border bg-v-callout-info text-code"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 16 16" class="inline shrink-0 mt-px h-5"><path fill="currentColor" d="M7.86 9.742a1 1 0 0 0-.08.1.5.5 0 0 0-.06.12.4.4 0 0 0-.04.12 1 1 0 0 0 0 .134.56.56 0 0 0 .053.253.6.6 0 0 0 .36.36.63.63 0 0 0 .507 0 .6.6 0 0 0 .36-.36.7.7 0 0 0 .04-.253.667.667 0 0 0-1.14-.474m.473-8.86a6.667 6.667 0 1 0 0 13.334 6.667 6.667 0 0 0 0-13.334m0 12a5.333 5.333 0 1 1 0-10.666 5.333 5.333 0 0 1 0 10.666m0-8.666a2 2 0 0 0-1.733 1 .667.667 0 1 0 1.153.666.667.667 0 0 1 1.052-.138.667.667 0 0 1-.472 1.138.667.667 0 0 0-.666.667v.667a.667.667 0 0 0 1.333 0v-.12a2 2 0 0 0-.667-3.88"></path></svg><div class="text-v-text"><p>The <code>event_time</code> from <code>system.query_log</code> and <code>start_datetime</code> from <code>pipe_stats_rt</code> may differ by a few milliseconds. Always join using <code>query_id</code> and <code>request_id</code> for accurate matching.</p></div></div><h2 id="extract-pipe-names-from-log-comment" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">Extract pipe names from log_comment<a class="headerlink" href="#extract-pipe-names-from-log-comment" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><p>Endpoint queries include metadata in the <code>log_comment</code> column as JSON. Extract the pipe name to filter by specific Endpoints:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-header"><div class="snippet-headerInfo overflow"><h5 class="snippet-title as-font--caption-bold as-cap overflow mr-4" title="Filter by Endpoint name">Filter by Endpoint name</h5></div></div><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT
    event_time,
    query_id,
    JSONExtractString(log_comment, &#x27;pipe&#x27;) as pipe_name,
    JSONExtractString(log_comment, &#x27;workspace&#x27;) as workspace,
    formatReadableSize(memory_usage) as memory_usage,
    query_duration_ms / 1000.0 as duration_seconds
FROM system.query_log
WHERE event_time &gt;= now() - INTERVAL 1 HOUR
    AND log_comment != &#x27;&#x27;
    AND JSONExtractString(log_comment, &#x27;pipe&#x27;) = &#x27;your_pipe_name&#x27;
    AND type = &#x27;QueryFinish&#x27;
ORDER BY event_time DESC
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>The <code>log_comment</code> JSON structure looks like:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">{&quot;workspace&quot;:&quot;prod&quot;,&quot;pipe&quot;:&quot;last_impressions__v7&quot;}
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h2 id="find-memory-intensive-endpoints" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">Find memory-intensive endpoints<a class="headerlink" href="#find-memory-intensive-endpoints" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><p>Identify which Endpoints consistently use the most memory:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-header"><div class="snippet-headerInfo overflow"><h5 class="snippet-title as-font--caption-bold as-cap overflow mr-4" title="Average memory by Endpoint">Average memory by Endpoint</h5></div></div><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT
    JSONExtractString(log_comment, &#x27;pipe&#x27;) as pipe_name,
    formatReadableSize(avg(memory_usage)) as avg_memory,
    formatReadableSize(max(memory_usage)) as max_memory,
    formatReadableSize(quantile(0.9)(memory_usage)) as p90_memory,
    count() as query_count
FROM system.query_log
WHERE event_time &gt;= now() - INTERVAL 24 HOUR
    AND type = &#x27;QueryFinish&#x27;
    AND log_comment != &#x27;&#x27;
GROUP BY pipe_name
ORDER BY avg(memory_usage) DESC
LIMIT 20
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h2 id="common-mistakes" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">Common mistakes<a class="headerlink" href="#common-mistakes" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><p>Avoid these common pitfalls when working with <code>system.query_log</code>:</p><h3 id="running-queries-without-time-filters" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Running queries without time filters<a class="headerlink" href="#running-queries-without-time-filters" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><div class="my-4 flex items-start gap-2 py-3 px-4 rounded border border-v-border"><div class="text-v-text"><p><strong>Never do this:</strong></p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT * FROM system.query_log
WHERE query LIKE &#x27;%my_datasource_id%&#x27;
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><p>This scans the entire table history and will timeout or take hundreds of seconds.</p></div></div><p><strong>Always include time filters:</strong></p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT * FROM system.query_log
WHERE event_time &gt;= now() - INTERVAL 1 HOUR
  AND query LIKE &#x27;%my_datasource_id%&#x27;
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h3 id="selecting-all-columns-with-select" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Selecting all columns with SELECT *<a class="headerlink" href="#selecting-all-columns-with-select" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>Avoid <code>SELECT *</code> in production queries. The <code>query</code> column can be very large, and many columns aren&#x27;t needed for most debugging tasks.</p><p><strong>Instead, select only what you need:</strong></p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">SELECT
    event_time,
    query_id,
    type,
    query_duration_ms,
    memory_usage,
    exception
FROM system.query_log
WHERE event_time &gt;= now() - INTERVAL 1 HOUR
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h3 id="forgetting-to-filter-by-query-type" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Forgetting to filter by query type<a class="headerlink" href="#forgetting-to-filter-by-query-type" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>When analyzing completed queries, include <code>type = &#x27;QueryFinish&#x27;</code> to exclude <code>QueryStart</code> entries and avoid counting queries twice:</p><div class="max-w-full overflow-auto mb-4"><div class="snippet"><div class="snippet-code-container"><div class="snippet-code is-visible"><pre class="cm-s-default">-- Without type filter: counts each query twice (Start + Finish)
SELECT count(*) FROM system.query_log
WHERE event_time &gt;= now() - INTERVAL 1 HOUR

-- With type filter: accurate count
SELECT count(*) FROM system.query_log
WHERE event_time &gt;= now() - INTERVAL 1 HOUR
  AND type = &#x27;QueryFinish&#x27;
</pre></div></div><div class="absolute top-0 right-0 p-2"><button class="snippet-copyButton"><svg class="" width="16" viewBox="0 0 16 16" fill="none" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg"><g opacity="1"><mask id="w-mask" fill="white"><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M13 3H7V9H13V3ZM7 2C6.44772 2 6 2.44772 6 3V9C6 9.55228 6.44772 10 7 10H13C13.5523 10 14 9.55228 14 9V3C14 2.44772 13.5523 2 13 2H7Z"></path></mask><path mask="url(#w-mask)" fill="#1FCC83" d="M7 3V2H6V3H7ZM13 3H14V2H13V3ZM7 9H6V10H7V9ZM13 9V10H14V9H13ZM7 4H13V2H7V4ZM8 9V3H6V9H8ZM13 8H7V10H13V8ZM12 3V9H14V3H12ZM7 3V1C5.89543 1 5 1.89543 5 3H7ZM7 9V3H5V9H7ZM7 9H5C5 10.1046 5.89543 11 7 11V9ZM13 9H7V11H13V9ZM13 9V11C14.1046 11 15 10.1046 15 9H13ZM13 3V9H15V3H13ZM13 3H15C15 1.89543 14.1046 1 13 1V3ZM7 3H13V1H7V3Z"></path><path fill-rule="evenodd" clip-rule="evenodd" d="M6 7H3V13H9V10H10V13C10 13.5523 9.55228 14 9 14H3C2.44772 14 2 13.5523 2 13V7C2 6.44772 2.44772 6 3 6H6V7Z" fill="#1FCC83"></path></g></svg></button></div></div></div><h3 id="using-overly-broad-time-windows" class="t-body-1 font-medium mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="8.0">Using overly broad time windows<a class="headerlink" href="#using-overly-broad-time-windows" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h3><p>Start with 1-hour windows and expand only if needed. A 24-hour query takes significantly longer than a 1-hour query:</p><ul><li><strong>1 hour</strong>: ~1-2 seconds</li><li><strong>24 hours</strong>: ~15-30 seconds</li><li><strong>7 days</strong>: May timeout or take minutes</li></ul><h2 id="best-practices" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">Best practices<a class="headerlink" href="#best-practices" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><p>When querying <code>system.query_log</code>, follow these guidelines:</p><ol><li><strong>Always filter by time</strong> - Use <code>event_time &gt;= now() - INTERVAL X HOUR</code> in every query</li><li><strong>Filter by query type</strong> - Add <code>AND type = &#x27;QueryFinish&#x27;</code> if you only need completed queries</li><li><strong>Limit your results</strong> - Use <code>LIMIT</code> to avoid processing unnecessary data</li><li><strong>Start small</strong> - Begin with 1-hour windows, then expand as needed</li><li><strong>Create monitoring Pipes</strong> - Turn useful debug queries into Endpoints for dashboards</li></ol><div class="my-4 flex items-start gap-2 py-3 px-4 rounded border border-v-border bg-v-callout-tip text-brand-dark"><svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" width="16" height="16" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 16 16" class="inline shrink-0 mt-px h-5"><path fill="currentColor" d="M11.393 1.88A5.33 5.33 0 0 0 6.94.773a5.33 5.33 0 0 0-4.18 4.214A5.38 5.38 0 0 0 3.907 9.42c.469.53.738 1.206.76 1.913v2a2 2 0 0 0 2 2h2.666a2 2 0 0 0 2-2V11.46c.023-.78.31-1.53.814-2.127a5.334 5.334 0 0 0-.754-7.466zM10 13.333a.667.667 0 0 1-.667.667H6.667A.667.667 0 0 1 6 13.333v-.666h4zm1.113-4.826A4.75 4.75 0 0 0 10 11.333H8.667v-2a.667.667 0 0 0-1.334 0v2H6A4.33 4.33 0 0 0 4.933 8.56a4 4 0 0 1 4.02-6.447A4 4 0 0 1 12 6c.005.913-.309 1.8-.887 2.507"></path></svg><div class="text-v-text"><p>Convert your most useful <code>system.query_log</code> queries into Pipes and expose them as Endpoints. This makes it easy to build real-time monitoring dashboards or set up alerts.</p></div></div><h2 id="next-steps" class="t-h4 font-semibold mt-10 mb-2" data-pagefind-weight="12.0">Next steps<a class="headerlink" href="#next-steps" title="Permalink to this heading" data-pagefind-ignore="true">¶</a></h2><ul><li>Learn how to <a href="./analyze-endpoints-performance">analyze Endpoint performance</a> using <code>tinybird.pipe_stats_rt</code></li><li>Monitor <a href="./jobs">Jobs</a> in your Workspace</li></ul></article><div class="flex items-center justify-end h-10" How to debug queries using system.query_log\nmeta:\n    description: Learn how to use system.query_log to debug slow queries, analyze memory usage, and troubleshoot issues in your Tinybird Workspace.\n---\n\n# How to debug queries using system.query_log\n\nWhen troubleshooting performance issues or investigating query failures, you often need execution details beyond what standard monitoring provides.  The `system.query_log` table is a native ClickHouse system table that records query execution at the database engine level beneath Tinybird. \nIt stores detailed information for every query executed in your Workspace, including execution time, memory usage, error codes, and failure reasons. For a complete description of available columns and data types, see the ClickHouse documentation on the [`system.query_log`](https://clickhouse.com/docs/operations/system-tables/query_log) table.\n\n{% callout type=\"info\" %}\n**When should I use system.query_log?**\n\nUse `system.query_log` when you need to:\n- Debug queries that are slower than expected\n- Investigate why specific queries are failing\n- Analyze memory consumption patterns\n- Track which Endpoints consume the most resources\n- Correlate query execution with Endpoint performance metrics\n\nFor routine monitoring of Endpoint performance, use [`tinybird.pipe_stats_rt`](./analyze-endpoints-performance) instead.\n{% /callout %}\n\nRead on to learn how to safely query `system.query_log` and use it to solve real-world debugging challenges.\n\n## Before you start\n\nThe `system.query_log` table is a ClickHouse system table that contains extensive historical data. Before querying it, understand:\n\n- How to [analyze Endpoint performance](./analyze-endpoints-performance) using `tinybird.pipe_stats_rt`\n- Basic SQL query patterns in Tinybird\n\n{% callout type=\"warning\" %}\nThe `system.query_log` table contains all historical query data. **Always filter by `event_time`** to avoid slow queries or timeouts. Queries without time filters can take hundreds of seconds or timeout completely. **Never run** `SELECT * FROM system.query_log` without filtering by time.\n{% /callout %}\n\n\n```sql {% title=\"Safe query pattern with 1-hour lookback\" %}\nSELECT *\nFROM system.query_log\nWHERE event_time \u003e= now() - INTERVAL 1 HOUR\n```\n\nStart with a 1-hour window (typically 1-2 seconds to execute) and expand the time range only if needed.\n\n## Understand query lifecycle\n\nEvery query in Tinybird generates two entries in `system.query_log`:\n\n1. **QueryStart** - Logged when query execution begins\n2. **QueryFinish** - Logged when the query completes successfully\n\nIf a query fails, you'll see a different type instead of `QueryFinish`:\n\n- **ExceptionBeforeStart** - Query failed before execution started (usually syntax errors)\n- **ExceptionWhileProcessing** - Query failed during execution (timeouts, memory exceeded, runtime errors)\n\nHere's how the query lifecycle flows:\n\n```\n┌─────────────────┐\n│  Query Begins   │\n└────────┬────────┘\n         │\n         ▼\n    QueryStart ──────────────────┐\n         │                       │\n         │                       │\n         ▼                       ▼\n┌─────────────────┐     ┌──────────────────────┐\n│ Query Executes  │     │  Syntax/Init Error   │\n└────────┬────────┘     └──────────┬───────────┘\n         │                         │\n         │                         ▼\n         │              ExceptionBeforeStart\n         │\n    ┌────┴────┐\n    │         │\n    ▼         ▼\n Success   Runtime Error\n    │         │\n    ▼         ▼\nQueryFinish   ExceptionWhileProcessing\n```\n\nThis two-entry pattern helps you distinguish between queries that are still running and those that have finished or failed.\n\n## Common debugging scenarios\n\n### Find slow queries\n\nIdentify queries taking longer than expected:\n\n```sql {% title=\"Queries taking more than 5 seconds\" %}\nSELECT\n    event_time,\n    query_id,\n    JSONExtractString(log_comment, 'pipe') as pipe_name,\n    query_duration_ms / 1000.0 as duration_seconds,\n    formatReadableSize(memory_usage) as peak_memory,\n    substring(query, 1, 100) as query_preview\nFROM system.query_log\nWHERE event_time \u003e= now() - INTERVAL 1 HOUR\n    AND type = 'QueryFinish'\n    AND query_duration_ms \u003e 5000\nORDER BY query_duration_ms DESC\nLIMIT 20\n```\n\nThis helps you identify performance bottlenecks in your Endpoints or scheduled operations.\n\n### Investigate query failures\n\nTrack which queries are failing and why:\n\n```sql {% title=\"Failed queries in the last hour\" %}\nSELECT\n    event_time,\n    query_id,\n    type,\n    JSONExtractString(log_comment, 'pipe') as pipe_name,\n    exception\nFROM system.query_log\nWHERE event_time \u003e= now() - INTERVAL 1 HOUR\n    AND type IN ('ExceptionBeforeStart', 'ExceptionWhileProcessing')\nORDER BY event_time DESC\n```\n\nThe `exception` column contains the error message, helping you quickly identify syntax errors, timeouts, or resource limits.\n\n### Analyze memory consumption\n\nFind queries consuming the most memory:\n\n```sql {% title=\"Memory-intensive queries\" %}\nSELECT\n    event_time,\n    query_id,\n    JSONExtractString(log_comment, 'pipe') as pipe_name,\n    formatReadableSize(memory_usage) as peak_memory,\n    query_duration_ms / 1000.0 as duration_seconds\nFROM system.query_log\nWHERE event_time \u003e= now() - INTERVAL 1 HOUR\n    AND type = 'QueryFinish'\nORDER BY memory_usage DESC\nLIMIT 20\n```\n\nThe `memory_usage` column shows peak memory in bytes. High memory usage may indicate opportunities for query optimization.\n\n### Track query failure rates\n\nMonitor how often queries are failing over time:\n\n```sql {% title=\"Query failures by hour\" %}\nSELECT\n    toStartOfHour(event_time) as hour,\n    type,\n    count() as failure_count\nFROM system.query_log\nWHERE event_time \u003e= now() - INTERVAL 24 HOUR\n    AND type IN ('ExceptionBeforeStart', 'ExceptionWhileProcessing')\nGROUP BY hour, type\nORDER BY hour DESC\n```\n\n## Connect query_log with Endpoint stats\n\nThe `query_id` in `system.query_log` matches the `request_id` from `tinybird.pipe_stats_rt`. This lets you combine high-level request metrics with detailed query execution data.\n\n```sql {% title=\"Combine endpoint stats with query details\" %}\nSELECT\n    ps.pipe_name,\n    ps.start_datetime,\n    ps.duration as request_duration,\n    formatReadableSize(ql.memory_usage) as query_memory,\n    ql.type as execution_status\nFROM tinybird.pipe_stats_rt ps\nJOIN system.query_log ql ON ps.request_id = ql.query_id\nWHERE ps.start_datetime \u003e= now() - INTERVAL 1 HOUR\n    AND ql.type = 'QueryFinish'\nORDER BY ps.start_datetime DESC\nLIMIT 100\n```\n\n{% callout type=\"info\" %}\nThe `event_time` from `system.query_log` and `start_datetime` from `pipe_stats_rt` may differ by a few milliseconds. Always join using `query_id` and `request_id` for accurate matching.\n{% /callout %}\n\n## Extract pipe names from log_comment\n\nEndpoint queries include metadata in the `log_comment` column as JSON. Extract the pipe name to filter by specific Endpoints:\n\n```sql {% title=\"Filter by Endpoint name\" %}\nSELECT\n    event_time,\n    query_id,\n    JSONExtractString(log_comment, 'pipe') as pipe_name,\n    JSONExtractString(log_comment, 'workspace') as workspace,\n    formatReadableSize(memory_usage) as memory_usage,\n    query_duration_ms / 1000.0 as duration_seconds\nFROM system.query_log\nWHERE event_time \u003e= now() - INTERVAL 1 HOUR\n    AND log_comment != ''\n    AND JSONExtractString(log_comment, 'pipe') = 'your_pipe_name'\n    AND type = 'QueryFinish'\nORDER BY event_time DESC\n```\n\nThe `log_comment` JSON structure looks like:\n\n```json\n{\"workspace\":\"prod\",\"pipe\":\"last_impressions__v7\"}\n```\n\n## Find memory-intensive endpoints\n\nIdentify which Endpoints consistently use the most memory:\n\n```sql {% title=\"Average memory by Endpoint\" %}\nSELECT\n    JSONExtractString(log_comment, 'pipe') as pipe_name,\n    formatReadableSize(avg(memory_usage)) as avg_memory,\n    formatReadableSize(max(memory_usage)) as max_memory,\n    formatReadableSize(quantile(0.9)(memory_usage)) as p90_memory,\n    count() as query_count\nFROM system.query_log\nWHERE event_time \u003e= now() - INTERVAL 24 HOUR\n    AND type = 'QueryFinish'\n    AND log_comment != ''\nGROUP BY pipe_name\nORDER BY avg(memory_usage) DESC\nLIMIT 20\n```\n\n## Common mistakes\n\nAvoid these common pitfalls when working with `system.query_log`:\n\n### Running queries without time filters\n\n{% callout type=\"danger\" %}\n**Never do this:**\n```sql\nSELECT * FROM system.query_log\nWHERE query LIKE '%my_datasource_id%'\n```\n\nThis scans the entire table history and will timeout or take hundreds of seconds.\n{% /callout %}\n\n**Always include time filters:**\n```sql\nSELECT * FROM system.query_log\nWHERE event_time \u003e= now() - INTERVAL 1 HOUR\n  AND query LIKE '%my_datasource_id%'\n```\n\n### Selecting all columns with SELECT *\n\nAvoid `SELECT *` in production queries. The `query` column can be very large, and many columns aren't needed for most debugging tasks.\n\n**Instead, select only what you need:**\n```sql\nSELECT\n    event_time,\n    query_id,\n    type,\n    query_duration_ms,\n    memory_usage,\n    exception\nFROM system.query_log\nWHERE event_time \u003e= now() - INTERVAL 1 HOUR\n```\n\n### Forgetting to filter by query type\n\nWhen analyzing completed queries, include `type = 'QueryFinish'` to exclude `QueryStart` entries and avoid counting queries twice:\n\n```sql\n-- Without type filter: counts each query twice (Start + Finish)\nSELECT count(*) FROM system.query_log\nWHERE event_time \u003e= now() - INTERVAL 1 HOUR\n\n-- With type filter: accurate count\nSELECT count(*) FROM system.query_log\nWHERE event_time \u003e= now() - INTERVAL 1 HOUR\n  AND type = 'QueryFinish'\n```\n\n### Using overly broad time windows\n\nStart with 1-hour windows and expand only if needed. A 24-hour query takes significantly longer than a 1-hour query:\n\n- **1 hour**: ~1-2 seconds\n- **24 hours**: ~15-30 seconds\n- **7 days**: May timeout or take minutes\n\n## Best practices\n\nWhen querying `system.query_log`, follow these guidelines:\n\n1. **Always filter by time** - Use `event_time \u003e= now() - INTERVAL X HOUR` in every query\n2. **Filter by query type** - Add `AND type = 'QueryFinish'` if you only need completed queries\n3. **Limit your results** - Use `LIMIT` to avoid processing unnecessary data\n4. **Start small** - Begin with 1-hour windows, then expand as needed\n5. **Create monitoring Pipes** - Turn useful debug queries into Endpoints for dashboards\n\n{% callout type=\"tip\" %}\nConvert your most useful `system.query_log` queries into Pipes and expose them as Endpoints. This makes it easy to build real-time monitoring dashboards or set up alerts.\n{% /callout %}\n\n## Next steps\n\n- Learn how to [analyze Endpoint performance](./analyze-endpoints-performance) using `tinybird.pipe_stats_rt`\n- Monitor [Jobs](./jobs) in your Workspace\n"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"2c:{\"fill\":\"currentColor\",\"d\":\"M7.86 9.742a1 1 0 0 0-.08.1.5.5 0 0 0-.06.12.4.4 0 0 0-.04.12 1 1 0 0 0 0 .134.56.56 0 0 0 .053.253.6.6 0 0 0 .36.36.63.63 0 0 0 .507 0 .6.6 0 0 0 .36-.36.7.7 0 0 0 .04-.253.667.667 0 0 0-1.14-.474m.473-8.86a6.667 6.667 0 1 0 0 13.334 6.667 6.667 0 0 0 0-13.334m0 12a5.333 5.333 0 1 1 0-10.666 5.333 5.333 0 0 1 0 10.666m0-8.666a2 2 0 0 0-1.733 1 .667.667 0 1 0 1.153.666.667.667 0 0 1 1.052-.138.667.667 0 0 1-.472 1.138.667.667 0 0 0-.666.667v.667a.667.667 0 0 0 1.333 0v-.12a2 2 0 0 0-.667-3.88\"}\n2b:[\"$\",\"path\",null,\"$2c\"]\n"])</script><script>self.__next_f.push([1,"8:[\"$\",\"div\",null,{\"className\":\"relative max-w-7xl mx-auto px-5 md:px-6 xl:grid xl:grid-cols-[1fr_280px]\",\"children\":[[\"$\",\"div\",null,{\"className\":\"max-w-4xl text-body md:px-4 md:pb-20 relative\",\"role\":\"main\",\"children\":[[\"$\",\"$L20\",null,{\"pageContent\":\"$21\",\"pagePath\":\"docs/monitoring/query-log\",\"children\":[\"$\",\"article\",null,{\"children\":[[\"$\",\"$L22\",null,{\"level\":1,\"name\":\"Heading\",\"children\":\"How to debug queries using system.query_log\"}],[\"$\",\"p\",null,{\"children\":[\"When troubleshooting performance issues or investigating query failures, you often need execution details beyond what standard monitoring provides.
